 (input bhashaa se) The Telangana Legislative Assembly on Saturday passed a bill making Telugu teaching and learning of Telugu language compulsory in state schools
 di telugana (vidhyalay main anivaary telugu shikshan evam siikhnaa) adhinium, 2018 kaa bijepi, tidipi, eimm or makapa samet sabhi dalon ne samarthan kiya
 The comments adhinium ke mutabik shaikshanik satr 2018-19 se shuru karte hue sabhi skulon main telugu ko kaksha pehali se dasvin tak charanbaddh tareeke se anivaary vishay banaaya jayega
 Deputy Chief Minister and Education Minister Kadiyam Srihari said that the purpose of this bill is to save and grow Telugu
 (input bhashaa se) According to the Act, Telugu will be made a compulsory subject in all schools in a phased manner from class i to X, starting from academic session 2018-19
 upmukhyamantri or shiksha mantri kadium srihari ne kaha ki is vidheyak kaa uddeshy telugu ko bachaana or badhanaa he
 (from input language) upmukhyamantri or shiksha mantri kadium srihari ne kaha ki is vidheyak kaa uddeshy telugu ko bachaana or badhanaa he
 (from input language) desh, duniya, mahanagar, khel, aarthik or bollywood main kya kuch hua

 1
 a small amount of fat is present in the water that is effective in reducing weight
 aise main agar aap vajan kam karnaa chaahate hai to ye ek bahut behatar vikalp sabit ho saktaa he

 2
